================



 Posted in **MTGO Standings**
 on June 26, 2022 










* [Bracket](#bracket)
* [Decklists](#decklists)
* [Standings](#standings)

Bracket
-------

**(4) Racerman, 2-1**






 (5) vihespanhol

### Finals






**(1) Oliver\_Hart, 2-0**
